new entry "MULTIATTACK_DRACONIC_SPIRIT"
type "StatusData"
data "StatusType" "BOOST"
data "DisplayName" "Multiattack"
data "Description" "Free attack after using an attack."
data "StackId" "MULTIATTACK_DRACONIC_SPIRIT"
data "Boosts" "UnlockSpellVariant(SpellId('Target_Rend'),ModifyUseCosts(Replace,ActionPoint,0,0,ActionPoint),ModifyIconGlow(),ModifyTooltipDescription())"
data "OnRemoveFunctors" "IF(RemoveCause(StatusRemoveCause.Condition) and HasPassive('Multiattack_DraconicSpirit_2',context.Source)):ApplyStatus(MULTIATTACK_DRACONIC_SPIRIT_2,100,1)"
